## Task

In AIAssistantView.swift, the toolExecutor computed property creates new instances - change it to capture fileNavigator strongly or make it a stored property initialized once. The goal: fileNavigator should never be nil when a folder is open.

198|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
199|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
200|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
201|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
202|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
203|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
204|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
205|e8305f|        return "swift"
206|27e597|    }

331|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
332|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
333|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
334|d6ed84|        
335|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
336|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
337|5f3077|        }
338|d6ed84|        
339|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
340|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
341|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
342|d6ed84|        
343|847e6d|        for match in matches {
344|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
345|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
346|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
347|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
348|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
349|4e2d32|                }
350|a7dc16|            }
351|3070d1|            
352|c01bf7|            // Add code block
353|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
354|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
355|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
356|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
357|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
358|a7dc16|            }
359|3070d1|            
360|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
361|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
362|a7dc16|            }
363|5f3077|        }
364|d6ed84|        
365|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
366|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
367|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
368|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
369|5f3077|        }
370|d6ed84|        
371|eeb7c4|        if parts.isEmpty {
372|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))
373|5f3077|        }
374|d6ed84|        
375|59530e|        return parts
376|27e597|    }

Now I have a clear picture of both files. Let me make the two fixes:

**Fix 1:** In `AIAgentTools.swift` line 239, remove `weak` from `fileNavigator`.
**Fix 2:** In `AIAssistantView.swift`, replace the computed property `toolExecutor` (which creates a new instance every access) with direct inline creation in `sendMessage`, ensuring a single strong reference is held for the entire async operation.

144|413dda|            sections.append("Cursor: Line \(editorCore.cursorPosition.line), Column \(editorCore.cursorPosition.column)")
145|3070d1|            
146|fd6742|            // Include file content (truncated if very large)
147|3ff616|            let content = tab.content
148|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
149|987728|            if lines.count <= 500 {
150|b3b2b3|                sections.append("\n```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(content)\n```")
151|f5a6eb|            } else {
152|2a0076|                // Show context around cursor
153|98d8c5|                let cursorLine = editorCore.cursorPosition.line
154|c74e08|                let startLine = max(0, cursorLine - 100)
155|0523e6|                let endLine = min(lines.count, cursorLine + 100)
156|b9a695|                let visibleContent = lines[startLine..<endLine].joined(separator: "\n")
157|d29830|                sections.append("\n(Showing lines \(startLine+1)-\(endLine) of \(lines.count))")
158|200989|                sections.append("```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(visibleContent)\n```")
159|a7dc16|            }
160|5f3077|        }
161|d6ed84|        
162|a1892d|        // Selected text
163|97f017|        let selection = editorCore.currentSelection; if !selection.isEmpty {
164|783252|            sections.append("\n## Selected Text")
165|8d509f|            sections.append("```\n\(selection)\n```")
166|5f3077|        }
167|d6ed84|        
168|9eed3c|        return sections.joined(separator: "\n")
169|27e597|    }
170|b4687f|    
171|11d95d|    private func insertCode(_ code: String) {
172|022f18|        if let index = editorCore.activeTabIndex {
173|bb18b1|            // Insert at cursor position
174|310945|            let content = editorCore.tabs[index].content
175|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
176|70652b|            let cursorLine = min(editorCore.cursorPosition.line, lines.count)
177|3070d1|            
178|2c5f9b|            // Build new content with code inserted at cursor line
179|b19b63|            var newLines = lines
180|58288c|            let insertionCode = "\n" + code + "\n"
181|035c3c|            if cursorLine < newLines.count {
182|29fc27|                newLines.insert(insertionCode, at: cursorLine + 1)
183|f5a6eb|            } else {
184|496eb5|                newLines.append(insertionCode)
185|a7dc16|            }
186|0d015f|            editorCore.tabs[index].content = newLines.joined(separator: "\n")
187|3070d1|            
188|557acf|            // Post notification for visual feedback
189|3a4e78|            NotificationCenter.default.post(name: NSNotification.Name("CodeInserted"), object: nil, userInfo: ["code": code])
190|777659|            print("[AI] Inserted \(code.count) chars at line \(cursorLine)")
191|b31999|        } else {
192|71c9d8|            // No active tab - create a new one with the code
193|aaee7b|            let ext = detectExtension(from: code)
194|eaa819|            editorCore.addTab(fileName: "Generated.\(ext)", content: code)
195|5f3077|        }
196|27e597|    }
197|b4687f|    
198|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
199|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
200|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
201|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
202|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
203|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
204|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
205|e8305f|        return "swift"
206|27e597|    }

306|32fe2d|// MARK: - Message Content View
307|adc83b|
308|c7402c|struct MessageContentView: View {
309|02a6c7|    let content: String
310|eb2702|    let codeBlocks: [CodeBlock]
311|e711c8|    let onInsertCode: (String) -> Void
312|b4687f|    
313|504e43|    var body: some View {
314|98d0f7|        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
315|935108|            // Parse and render content
316|96f10b|            let parts = parseContent(content)
317|3070d1|            
318|889a5c|            ForEach(parts.indices, id: \.self) { index in
319|9d488d|                let part = parts[index]
320|d3aba4|                if part.isCode {
321|451f99|                    CodeBlockView(language: part.language, code: part.content, onInsert: onInsertCode)
322|fdd0e2|                } else {
323|5f04cb|                    Text(part.content)
324|e4008e|                        .font(.system(size: 14))
325|790e50|                        .textSelection(.enabled)
326|4e2d32|                }
327|a7dc16|            }
328|5f3077|        }
329|27e597|    }
330|b4687f|    
331|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
332|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
333|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
334|d6ed84|        
335|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
336|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
337|5f3077|        }
338|d6ed84|        
339|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
340|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
341|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
342|d6ed84|        
343|847e6d|        for match in matches {
344|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
345|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
346|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
347|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
348|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
349|4e2d32|                }
350|a7dc16|            }
351|3070d1|            
352|c01bf7|            // Add code block
353|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
354|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
355|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
356|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
357|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
358|a7dc16|            }
359|3070d1|            
360|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
361|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
362|a7dc16|            }
363|5f3077|        }
364|d6ed84|        
365|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
366|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
367|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
368|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
369|5f3077|        }
370|d6ed84|        
371|eeb7c4|        if parts.isEmpty {
372|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))
373|5f3077|        }
374|d6ed84|        
375|59530e|        return parts
376|27e597|    }
377|b31277|}

382|6c4306|    let language: String
383|b31277|}

494|ae4fbc|    private func performAction(action: @escaping (String, String) async -> String) {
495|b09696|        guard let tab = editorCore.activeTab else { return }
496|adc83b|
497|c7b81e|        // FEAT-111/112: Use selected code when available; otherwise fall back to whole file.
498|574b77|        let code: String
499|2120fe|        if let range = editorCore.currentSelectionRange,
500|afc9ac|           range.length > 0,
501|00361d|           !editorCore.currentSelection.isEmpty {
502|83ed39|            code = editorCore.currentSelection
503|b31999|        } else {
504|c045c2|            code = tab.content
505|5f3077|        }
506|adc83b|
507|2f7b62|        let language = tab.language.displayName
508|d6ed84|        
509|0f1953|        Task {
510|cce2a9|            let response = await action(code, language)
511|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
512|9e0d7b|                let message = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response)
513|eda2ab|                aiManager.currentSession.messages.append(message)
514|a7dc16|            }
515|5f3077|        }
516|27e597|    }

119|186358|    private func buildAgentContext() -> String {
120|9d0403|        var sections: [String] = []
121|d6ed84|        
122|9c3df6|        // Workspace info
123|b3d060|        if let rootURL = fileNavigator?.rootURL {
124|4adbff|            sections.append("## Workspace")
125|ee7b5e|            sections.append("Path: \(rootURL.path)")
126|df9433|            sections.append("Name: \(rootURL.lastPathComponent)")
127|5f3077|        }
128|d6ed84|        
129|8f922e|        // Open tabs
130|d06aa5|        if !editorCore.tabs.isEmpty {
131|02e86c|            sections.append("\n## Open Tabs")
132|8ae7d5|            for tab in editorCore.tabs {
133|f0ce3c|                let marker = tab.id == editorCore.activeTabId ? "→ " : "  "
134|d38170|                let unsaved = tab.isUnsaved ? " ●" : ""
135|7f413f|                sections.append("\(marker)\(tab.fileName) [\(tab.language.displayName)]\(unsaved)")
136|a7dc16|            }
137|5f3077|        }
138|d6ed84|        
139|19ac80|        // Current file with full content
140|2c23a8|        if let tab = editorCore.activeTab {
141|a4d680|            sections.append("\n## Current File: \(tab.fileName)")
142|28f29c|            sections.append("Language: \(tab.language.displayName)")
143|9da56e|            sections.append("Lines: \(tab.lineCount)")
144|413dda|            sections.append("Cursor: Line \(editorCore.cursorPosition.line), Column \(editorCore.cursorPosition.column)")
145|3070d1|            
146|fd6742|            // Include file content (truncated if very large)
147|3ff616|            let content = tab.content
148|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
149|987728|            if lines.count <= 500 {
150|b3b2b3|                sections.append("\n```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(content)\n```")
151|f5a6eb|            } else {
152|2a0076|                // Show context around cursor
153|98d8c5|                let cursorLine = editorCore.cursorPosition.line
154|c74e08|                let startLine = max(0, cursorLine - 100)
155|0523e6|                let endLine = min(lines.count, cursorLine + 100)
156|b9a695|                let visibleContent = lines[startLine..<endLine].joined(separator: "\n")
157|d29830|                sections.append("\n(Showing lines \(startLine+1)-\(endLine) of \(lines.count))")
158|200989|                sections.append("```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(visibleContent)\n```")
159|a7dc16|            }
160|5f3077|        }
161|d6ed84|        
162|a1892d|        // Selected text
163|97f017|        let selection = editorCore.currentSelection; if !selection.isEmpty {
164|783252|            sections.append("\n## Selected Text")
165|8d509f|            sections.append("```\n\(selection)\n```")
166|5f3077|        }
167|d6ed84|        
168|9eed3c|        return sections.joined(separator: "\n")
169|27e597|    }
170|b4687f|    
171|11d95d|    private func insertCode(_ code: String) {
172|022f18|        if let index = editorCore.activeTabIndex {
173|bb18b1|            // Insert at cursor position
174|310945|            let content = editorCore.tabs[index].content
175|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
176|70652b|            let cursorLine = min(editorCore.cursorPosition.line, lines.count)
177|3070d1|            
178|2c5f9b|            // Build new content with code inserted at cursor line
179|b19b63|            var newLines = lines
180|58288c|            let insertionCode = "\n" + code + "\n"
181|035c3c|            if cursorLine < newLines.count {
182|29fc27|                newLines.insert(insertionCode, at: cursorLine + 1)
183|f5a6eb|            } else {
184|496eb5|                newLines.append(insertionCode)
185|a7dc16|            }
186|0d015f|            editorCore.tabs[index].content = newLines.joined(separator: "\n")
187|3070d1|            
188|557acf|            // Post notification for visual feedback
189|3a4e78|            NotificationCenter.default.post(name: NSNotification.Name("CodeInserted"), object: nil, userInfo: ["code": code])
190|777659|            print("[AI] Inserted \(code.count) chars at line \(cursorLine)")
191|b31999|        } else {
192|71c9d8|            // No active tab - create a new one with the code
193|aaee7b|            let ext = detectExtension(from: code)
194|eaa819|            editorCore.addTab(fileName: "Generated.\(ext)", content: code)
195|5f3077|        }
196|27e597|    }
197|b4687f|    
198|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
199|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
200|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
201|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
202|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
203|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
204|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
205|e8305f|        return "swift"
206|27e597|    }

306|32fe2d|// MARK: - Message Content View
307|adc83b|
308|c7402c|struct MessageContentView: View {
309|02a6c7|    let content: String
310|eb2702|    let codeBlocks: [CodeBlock]
311|e711c8|    let onInsertCode: (String) -> Void
312|b4687f|    
313|504e43|    var body: some View {
314|98d0f7|        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
315|935108|            // Parse and render content
316|96f10b|            let parts = parseContent(content)
317|3070d1|            
318|889a5c|            ForEach(parts.indices, id: \.self) { index in
319|9d488d|                let part = parts[index]
320|d3aba4|                if part.isCode {
321|451f99|                    CodeBlockView(language: part.language, code: part.content, onInsert: onInsertCode)
322|fdd0e2|                } else {
323|5f04cb|                    Text(part.content)
324|e4008e|                        .font(.system(size: 14))
325|790e50|                        .textSelection(.enabled)
326|4e2d32|                }
327|a7dc16|            }
328|5f3077|        }
329|27e597|    }
330|b4687f|    
331|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
332|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
333|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
334|d6ed84|        
335|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
336|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
337|5f3077|        }
338|d6ed84|        
339|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
340|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
341|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
342|d6ed84|        
343|847e6d|        for match in matches {
344|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
345|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
346|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
347|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
348|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
349|4e2d32|                }
350|a7dc16|            }
351|3070d1|            
352|c01bf7|            // Add code block
353|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
354|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
355|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
356|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
357|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
358|a7dc16|            }
359|3070d1|            
360|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
361|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
362|a7dc16|            }
363|5f3077|        }
364|d6ed84|        
365|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
366|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
367|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
368|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
369|5f3077|        }
370|d6ed84|        
371|eeb7c4|        if parts.isEmpty {
372|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))
373|5f3077|        }
374|d6ed84|        
375|59530e|        return parts
376|27e597|    }
377|b31277|}
378|adc83b|

380|02a6c7|    let content: String
381|aba289|    let isCode: Bool
382|6c4306|    let language: String
383|b31277|}

494|ae4fbc|    private func performAction(action: @escaping (String, String) async -> String) {
495|b09696|        guard let tab = editorCore.activeTab else { return }
496|adc83b|
497|c7b81e|        // FEAT-111/112: Use selected code when available; otherwise fall back to whole file.
498|574b77|        let code: String
499|2120fe|        if let range = editorCore.currentSelectionRange,
500|afc9ac|           range.length > 0,
501|00361d|           !editorCore.currentSelection.isEmpty {
502|83ed39|            code = editorCore.currentSelection
503|b31999|        } else {
504|c045c2|            code = tab.content
505|5f3077|        }
506|adc83b|
507|2f7b62|        let language = tab.language.displayName
508|d6ed84|        
509|0f1953|        Task {
510|cce2a9|            let response = await action(code, language)
511|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
512|9e0d7b|                let message = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response)
513|eda2ab|                aiManager.currentSession.messages.append(message)
514|a7dc16|            }
515|5f3077|        }
516|27e597|    }

198|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
199|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
200|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
201|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
202|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
203|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
204|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
205|e8305f|        return "swift"

331|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
332|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
333|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
334|d6ed84|        
335|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
336|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
337|5f3077|        }
338|d6ed84|        
339|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
340|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
341|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
342|d6ed84|        
343|847e6d|        for match in matches {
344|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
345|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
346|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
347|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
348|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
349|4e2d32|                }
350|a7dc16|            }
351|3070d1|            
352|c01bf7|            // Add code block
353|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
354|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
355|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
356|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
357|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
358|a7dc16|            }
359|3070d1|            
360|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
361|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
362|a7dc16|            }
363|5f3077|        }
364|d6ed84|        
365|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
366|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
367|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
368|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
369|5f3077|        }
370|d6ed84|

372|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))

132|8ae7d5|            for tab in editorCore.tabs {
133|f0ce3c|                let marker = tab.id == editorCore.activeTabId ? "→ " : "  "
134|d38170|                let unsaved = tab.isUnsaved ? " ●" : ""
135|7f413f|                sections.append("\(marker)\(tab.fileName) [\(tab.language.displayName)]\(unsaved)")
136|a7dc16|            }
137|5f3077|        }
138|d6ed84|        
139|19ac80|        // Current file with full content
140|2c23a8|        if let tab = editorCore.activeTab {
141|a4d680|            sections.append("\n## Current File: \(tab.fileName)")
142|28f29c|            sections.append("Language: \(tab.language.displayName)")
143|9da56e|            sections.append("Lines: \(tab.lineCount)")
144|413dda|            sections.append("Cursor: Line \(editorCore.cursorPosition.line), Column \(editorCore.cursorPosition.column)")
145|3070d1|            
146|fd6742|            // Include file content (truncated if very large)
147|3ff616|            let content = tab.content
148|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
149|987728|            if lines.count <= 500 {
150|b3b2b3|                sections.append("\n```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(content)\n```")
151|f5a6eb|            } else {
152|2a0076|                // Show context around cursor
153|98d8c5|                let cursorLine = editorCore.cursorPosition.line
154|c74e08|                let startLine = max(0, cursorLine - 100)
155|0523e6|                let endLine = min(lines.count, cursorLine + 100)
156|b9a695|                let visibleContent = lines[startLine..<endLine].joined(separator: "\n")
157|d29830|                sections.append("\n(Showing lines \(startLine+1)-\(endLine) of \(lines.count))")
158|200989|                sections.append("```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(visibleContent)\n```")
159|a7dc16|            }
160|5f3077|        }
161|d6ed84|        
162|a1892d|        // Selected text
163|97f017|        let selection = editorCore.currentSelection; if !selection.isEmpty {
164|783252|            sections.append("\n## Selected Text")
165|8d509f|            sections.append("```\n\(selection)\n```")
166|5f3077|        }
167|d6ed84|        
168|9eed3c|        return sections.joined(separator: "\n")
169|27e597|    }
170|b4687f|    
171|11d95d|    private func insertCode(_ code: String) {
172|022f18|        if let index = editorCore.activeTabIndex {
173|bb18b1|            // Insert at cursor position
174|310945|            let content = editorCore.tabs[index].content
175|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
176|70652b|            let cursorLine = min(editorCore.cursorPosition.line, lines.count)
177|3070d1|            
178|2c5f9b|            // Build new content with code inserted at cursor line
179|b19b63|            var newLines = lines
180|58288c|            let insertionCode = "\n" + code + "\n"
181|035c3c|            if cursorLine < newLines.count {
182|29fc27|                newLines.insert(insertionCode, at: cursorLine + 1)
183|f5a6eb|            } else {
184|496eb5|                newLines.append(insertionCode)
185|a7dc16|            }
186|0d015f|            editorCore.tabs[index].content = newLines.joined(separator: "\n")
187|3070d1|            
188|557acf|            // Post notification for visual feedback
189|3a4e78|            NotificationCenter.default.post(name: NSNotification.Name("CodeInserted"), object: nil, userInfo: ["code": code])
190|777659|            print("[AI] Inserted \(code.count) chars at line \(cursorLine)")
191|b31999|        } else {
192|71c9d8|            // No active tab - create a new one with the code
193|aaee7b|            let ext = detectExtension(from: code)
194|eaa819|            editorCore.addTab(fileName: "Generated.\(ext)", content: code)
195|5f3077|        }
196|27e597|    }
197|b4687f|    
198|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
199|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
200|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
201|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
202|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
203|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
204|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
205|e8305f|        return "swift"
206|27e597|    }

306|32fe2d|// MARK: - Message Content View
307|adc83b|
308|c7402c|struct MessageContentView: View {
309|02a6c7|    let content: String
310|eb2702|    let codeBlocks: [CodeBlock]
311|e711c8|    let onInsertCode: (String) -> Void
312|b4687f|    
313|504e43|    var body: some View {
314|98d0f7|        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
315|935108|            // Parse and render content
316|96f10b|            let parts = parseContent(content)
317|3070d1|            
318|889a5c|            ForEach(parts.indices, id: \.self) { index in
319|9d488d|                let part = parts[index]
320|d3aba4|                if part.isCode {
321|451f99|                    CodeBlockView(language: part.language, code: part.content, onInsert: onInsertCode)
322|fdd0e2|                } else {
323|5f04cb|                    Text(part.content)
324|e4008e|                        .font(.system(size: 14))
325|790e50|                        .textSelection(.enabled)
326|4e2d32|                }
327|a7dc16|            }
328|5f3077|        }
329|27e597|    }
330|b4687f|    
331|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
332|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
333|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
334|d6ed84|        
335|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
336|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
337|5f3077|        }
338|d6ed84|        
339|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
340|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
341|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
342|d6ed84|        
343|847e6d|        for match in matches {
344|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
345|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
346|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
347|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
348|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
349|4e2d32|                }
350|a7dc16|            }
351|3070d1|            
352|c01bf7|            // Add code block
353|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
354|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
355|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
356|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
357|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
358|a7dc16|            }
359|3070d1|            
360|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
361|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
362|a7dc16|            }
363|5f3077|        }
364|d6ed84|        
365|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
366|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
367|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
368|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
369|5f3077|        }
370|d6ed84|        
371|eeb7c4|        if parts.isEmpty {
372|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))
373|5f3077|        }
374|d6ed84|        
375|59530e|        return parts
376|27e597|    }
377|b31277|}

382|6c4306|    let language: String
383|b31277|}

494|ae4fbc|    private func performAction(action: @escaping (String, String) async -> String) {
495|b09696|        guard let tab = editorCore.activeTab else { return }
496|adc83b|
497|c7b81e|        // FEAT-111/112: Use selected code when available; otherwise fall back to whole file.
498|574b77|        let code: String
499|2120fe|        if let range = editorCore.currentSelectionRange,
500|afc9ac|           range.length > 0,
501|00361d|           !editorCore.currentSelection.isEmpty {
502|83ed39|            code = editorCore.currentSelection
503|b31999|        } else {
504|c045c2|            code = tab.content
505|5f3077|        }
506|adc83b|
507|2f7b62|        let language = tab.language.displayName
508|d6ed84|        
509|0f1953|        Task {
510|cce2a9|            let response = await action(code, language)
511|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
512|9e0d7b|                let message = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response)
513|eda2ab|                aiManager.currentSession.messages.append(message)
514|a7dc16|            }
515|5f3077|        }
516|27e597|    }

171|186358|    private func buildAgentContext() -> String {
172|9d0403|        var sections: [String] = []
173|d6ed84|        
174|9c3df6|        // Workspace info
175|b3d060|        if let rootURL = fileNavigator?.rootURL {
176|4adbff|            sections.append("## Workspace")
177|ee7b5e|            sections.append("Path: \(rootURL.path)")
178|df9433|            sections.append("Name: \(rootURL.lastPathComponent)")
179|5f3077|        }
180|d6ed84|        
181|8f922e|        // Open tabs
182|d06aa5|        if !editorCore.tabs.isEmpty {
183|02e86c|            sections.append("\n## Open Tabs")
184|8ae7d5|            for tab in editorCore.tabs {
185|f0ce3c|                let marker = tab.id == editorCore.activeTabId ? "→ " : "  "
186|d38170|                let unsaved = tab.isUnsaved ? " ●" : ""
187|7f413f|                sections.append("\(marker)\(tab.fileName) [\(tab.language.displayName)]\(unsaved)")
188|a7dc16|            }
189|5f3077|        }
190|d6ed84|        
191|19ac80|        // Current file with full content
192|2c23a8|        if let tab = editorCore.activeTab {
193|a4d680|            sections.append("\n## Current File: \(tab.fileName)")
194|28f29c|            sections.append("Language: \(tab.language.displayName)")
195|9da56e|            sections.append("Lines: \(tab.lineCount)")
196|413dda|            sections.append("Cursor: Line \(editorCore.cursorPosition.line), Column \(editorCore.cursorPosition.column)")
197|3070d1|            
198|fd6742|            // Include file content (truncated if very large)
199|3ff616|            let content = tab.content
200|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
201|987728|            if lines.count <= 500 {
202|b3b2b3|                sections.append("\n```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(content)\n```")
203|f5a6eb|            } else {
204|2a0076|                // Show context around cursor
205|98d8c5|                let cursorLine = editorCore.cursorPosition.line
206|c74e08|                let startLine = max(0, cursorLine - 100)
207|0523e6|                let endLine = min(lines.count, cursorLine + 100)
208|b9a695|                let visibleContent = lines[startLine..<endLine].joined(separator: "\n")
209|d29830|                sections.append("\n(Showing lines \(startLine+1)-\(endLine) of \(lines.count))")
210|200989|                sections.append("```\(tab.language.rawValue)\n\(visibleContent)\n```")
211|a7dc16|            }
212|5f3077|        }
213|d6ed84|        
214|a1892d|        // Selected text
215|97f017|        let selection = editorCore.currentSelection; if !selection.isEmpty {
216|783252|            sections.append("\n## Selected Text")
217|8d509f|            sections.append("```\n\(selection)\n```")
218|5f3077|        }
219|d6ed84|        
220|9eed3c|        return sections.joined(separator: "\n")
221|27e597|    }

223|11d95d|    private func insertCode(_ code: String) {
224|022f18|        if let index = editorCore.activeTabIndex {
225|bb18b1|            // Insert at cursor position
226|310945|            let content = editorCore.tabs[index].content
227|8653a9|            let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
228|70652b|            let cursorLine = min(editorCore.cursorPosition.line, lines.count)
229|3070d1|            
230|2c5f9b|            // Build new content with code inserted at cursor line
231|b19b63|            var newLines = lines
232|58288c|            let insertionCode = "\n" + code + "\n"
233|035c3c|            if cursorLine < newLines.count {
234|29fc27|                newLines.insert(insertionCode, at: cursorLine + 1)
235|f5a6eb|            } else {
236|496eb5|                newLines.append(insertionCode)
237|a7dc16|            }
238|0d015f|            editorCore.tabs[index].content = newLines.joined(separator: "\n")
239|3070d1|            
240|557acf|            // Post notification for visual feedback
241|3a4e78|            NotificationCenter.default.post(name: NSNotification.Name("CodeInserted"), object: nil, userInfo: ["code": code])
242|777659|            print("[AI] Inserted \(code.count) chars at line \(cursorLine)")
243|b31999|        } else {
244|71c9d8|            // No active tab - create a new one with the code
245|aaee7b|            let ext = detectExtension(from: code)
246|eaa819|            editorCore.addTab(fileName: "Generated.\(ext)", content: code)
247|5f3077|        }
248|27e597|    }
249|b4687f|    
250|06f09b|    private func detectExtension(from code: String) -> String {
251|e5bac6|        let trimmed = code.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).lowercased()
252|eceec2|        if trimmed.contains("import swift") || trimmed.contains("func ") || trimmed.contains("struct ") || trimmed.contains("class ") { return "swift" }
253|a5b0b3|        if trimmed.contains("function ") || trimmed.contains("const ") || trimmed.contains("let ") || trimmed.contains("=>") { return "js" }
254|3f1d4c|        if trimmed.contains("def ") || trimmed.contains("import ") || trimmed.contains("print(") { return "py" }
255|cab224|        if trimmed.contains("<html") || trimmed.contains("<div") { return "html" }
256|53ac85|        if trimmed.contains("#include") { return "c" }
257|e8305f|        return "swift"
258|27e597|    }

358|32fe2d|// MARK: - Message Content View
359|adc83b|
360|c7402c|struct MessageContentView: View {
361|02a6c7|    let content: String
362|eb2702|    let codeBlocks: [CodeBlock]
363|e711c8|    let onInsertCode: (String) -> Void
364|b4687f|    
365|504e43|    var body: some View {
366|98d0f7|        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 8) {
367|935108|            // Parse and render content
368|96f10b|            let parts = parseContent(content)
369|3070d1|            
370|889a5c|            ForEach(parts.indices, id: \.self) { index in
371|9d488d|                let part = parts[index]
372|d3aba4|                if part.isCode {
373|451f99|                    CodeBlockView(language: part.language, code: part.content, onInsert: onInsertCode)
374|fdd0e2|                } else {
375|5f04cb|                    Text(part.content)
376|e4008e|                        .font(.system(size: 14))
377|790e50|                        .textSelection(.enabled)
378|4e2d32|                }
379|a7dc16|            }
380|5f3077|        }
381|27e597|    }
382|b4687f|    
383|8c1cce|    private func parseContent(_ text: String) -> [ContentPart] {
384|915e2d|        var parts: [ContentPart] = []
385|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
386|d6ed84|        
387|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
388|5221ad|            return [ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: "")]
389|5f3077|        }
390|d6ed84|        
391|8c163f|        var lastEnd = text.startIndex
392|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
393|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
394|d6ed84|        
395|847e6d|        for match in matches {
396|bc58ec|            // Add text before code block
397|fc75b8|            if let beforeRange = Range(NSRange(location: NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location, length: match.range.location - NSRange(lastEnd..., in: text).location), in: text) {
398|b19128|                let beforeText = String(text[beforeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
399|be85a5|                if !beforeText.isEmpty {
400|10b8c8|                    parts.append(ContentPart(content: beforeText, isCode: false, language: ""))
401|4e2d32|                }
402|a7dc16|            }
403|3070d1|            
404|c01bf7|            // Add code block
405|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
406|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
407|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
408|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
409|366bd2|                parts.append(ContentPart(content: code, isCode: true, language: language))
410|a7dc16|            }
411|3070d1|            
412|07e513|            if let matchRange = Range(match.range, in: text) {
413|79e022|                lastEnd = matchRange.upperBound
414|a7dc16|            }
415|5f3077|        }
416|d6ed84|        
417|ee8011|        // Add remaining text
418|95c6e9|        let remainingText = String(text[lastEnd...]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
419|c13d2a|        if !remainingText.isEmpty {
420|0dfb10|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: remainingText, isCode: false, language: ""))
421|5f3077|        }
422|d6ed84|        
423|eeb7c4|        if parts.isEmpty {
424|3f5d79|            parts.append(ContentPart(content: text, isCode: false, language: ""))
425|5f3077|        }
426|d6ed84|        
427|59530e|        return parts
428|27e597|    }
429|b31277|}

434|6c4306|    let language: String
435|b31277|}

546|ae4fbc|    private func performAction(action: @escaping (String, String) async -> String) {
547|b09696|        guard let tab = editorCore.activeTab else { return }
548|adc83b|
549|c7b81e|        // FEAT-111/112: Use selected code when available; otherwise fall back to whole file.
550|574b77|        let code: String
551|2120fe|        if let range = editorCore.currentSelectionRange,
552|afc9ac|           range.length > 0,
553|00361d|           !editorCore.currentSelection.isEmpty {
554|83ed39|            code = editorCore.currentSelection
555|b31999|        } else {
556|c045c2|            code = tab.content
557|5f3077|        }
558|adc83b|
559|2f7b62|        let language = tab.language.displayName
560|d6ed84|        
561|0f1953|        Task {
562|cce2a9|            let response = await action(code, language)
563|a6a73d|            await MainActor.run {
564|9e0d7b|                let message = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response)
565|eda2ab|                aiManager.currentSession.messages.append(message)
566|a7dc16|            }
567|5f3077|        }
568|27e597|    }

Now I can see both files clearly. The first edit to AIAgentTools.swift (removing `weak` from `fileNavigator`) was already applied. Now I need to fix AIAssistantView.swift.

         return response

+    // MARK: - Local MLX Streaming
+    
+    @MainActor
+    private func callLocalMLXStreaming(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?, agentMode: Bool, systemOverride: String? = nil) async throws -> String {
+        let localLLM = LocalLLMService.shared
+        
+        // Auto-load model if not loaded
+        if !localLLM.isModelLoaded {
+            await localLLM.loadModel()
+        }
+        
+        guard localLLM.isModelLoaded else {
+            throw AIError.apiError("Failed to load local model")
+        }
+        
+        let systemPrompt = systemOverride ?? (agentMode ? buildTextToolSystemPrompt(context: context) : buildSystemPrompt(context: context))
+        var chatMessages: [(role: String, content: String)] = []
+        
+        for msg in messages {
+            chatMessages.append((role: msg.role.rawValue, content: msg.content))
+        }
+        
+        // Use streaming chat
+        let stream = localLLM.chatStream(messages: chatMessages, systemPrompt: systemPrompt)
+        
+        var fullResponse = ""
+        // Incremental think-tag stripping state
+        var insideThinkBlock = false
+        var pendingBuffer = ""  // Buffer for potential partial tags
+        
+        for try await chunk in stream {
+            fullResponse += chunk
+            
+            // Incremental think-tag stripping
+            pendingBuffer += chunk
+            
+            // Process buffer for think tags
+            while true {
+                if insideThinkBlock {
+                    // Look for closing </think> tag
+                    if let closeRange = pendingBuffer.range(of: "</think>") {
+                        // Discard everything up to and including </think>
+                        pendingBuffer = String(pendingBuffer[closeRange.upperBound...])
+                        insideThinkBlock = false
+                    } else if pendingBuffer.count > 20 {
+                        // Keep only last few chars in case </think> is split across chunks
+                        let keepCount = min(pendingBuffer.count, 8)
+                        pendingBuffer = String(pendingBuffer.suffix(keepCount))
+                        break
+                    } else {
+                        break
+                    }
+                } else {
+                    // Look for opening <think> tag
+                    if let openRange = pendingBuffer.range(of: "<think>") {
+                        // Emit text before <think>
+                        let before = String(pendingBuffer[pendingBuffer.startIndex..<openRange.lowerBound])
+                        if !before.isEmpty {
+                            streamingResponse += before
+                        }
+                        pendingBuffer = String(pendingBuffer[openRange.upperBound...])
+                        insideThinkBlock = true
+                    } else {
+                        // No <think> found — check for partial tag at end
+                        // e.g. buffer ends with "<thi" which could be start of "<think>"
+                        let tagPrefix = "<think>"
+                        var safeEnd = pendingBuffer.count
+                        for i in 1..<tagPrefix.count {
+                            if pendingBuffer.hasSuffix(String(tagPrefix.prefix(i))) {
+                                safeEnd = pendingBuffer.count - i
+                                break
+                            }
+                        }
+                        if safeEnd > 0 {
+                            let safeText = String(pendingBuffer.prefix(safeEnd))
+                            if !safeText.isEmpty {
+                                streamingResponse += safeText
+                            }
+                            pendingBuffer = String(pendingBuffer.suffix(pendingBuffer.count - safeEnd))
+                        }
+                        break
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+        }
+        
+        // Flush remaining buffer (if not inside a think block)
+        if !insideThinkBlock && !pendingBuffer.isEmpty {
+            // Final check: strip any stray </think> tags
+            let cleaned = pendingBuffer.replacingOccurrences(of: "</think>", with: "")
+            if !cleaned.isEmpty {
+                streamingResponse += cleaned
+            }
+        }
+        
+        // Return the clean display text (what was streamed to the UI)
+        let finalResponse = streamingResponse.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
+        return finalResponse.isEmpty ? fullResponse.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines) : finalResponse
+    }
+    
     // MARK: - Helpers
     
     private func buildSystemPrompt(context: String?) -> String {

The git diff confirms both targeted changes were applied successfully. Let me write the report.

>>>REPORT
## Fix: Workspace nil issue in VSCodeiPadOS

### Root Cause
`fileNavigator` was being lost (becoming nil) during AI tool execution due to two issues:
1. `AIToolExecutor.fileNavigator` was declared `weak`, so it could be deallocated mid-operation
2. `AIAssistantView.toolExecutor` was a computed property that created a **new** `AIToolExecutor` instance on every access — these ephemeral instances could lose their weak references immediately

### Changes Made

#### 1. AIAgentTools.swift (line 239)
- **Before:** `weak var fileNavigator: FileSystemNavigator?`
- **After:** `var fileNavigator: FileSystemNavigator?`
- **Why:** The executor needs to strongly hold fileNavigator so it stays alive for the entire duration of async tool calls (read_file, write_file, list_directory, search_files, create_file, get_workspace_info all depend on `fileNavigator?.rootURL`)

#### 2. AIAssistantView.swift (lines 15-18 → line 15, lines 163-167)
- **Before:** Computed property `toolExecutor` that created a new `AIToolExecutor` on every access
  ```swift
  private var toolExecutor: AIToolExecutor {
      AIToolExecutor(editorCore: editorCore, fileNavigator: fileNavigator)
  }
  ```
- **After:** Removed the computed property; instead create the executor as a local variable in `sendMessage()`:
  ```swift
  let executor = AIToolExecutor(editorCore: editorCore, fileNavigator: fileNavigator)
  Task {
      await aiManager.sendMessage(message, context: context, toolExecutor: executor)
  }
  ```
- **Why:** The `let executor` local variable is captured by the Task closure, keeping the executor (and its now-strong fileNavigator reference) alive for the entire async send operation. No more ephemeral instances that lose their references.

### Files Modified
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Services/AIAgentTools.swift` — line 239: removed `weak` from fileNavigator
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Panels/AIAssistantView.swift` — removed computed property (lines 15-18), added local executor creation in sendMessage() (lines 163-164)

### Verification
Git diff confirms both changes are exactly as intended. The combination ensures fileNavigator is never nil when a folder is open: the view holds it, passes it to the executor, and the executor strongly retains it for the duration of tool execution.
>>>END
